],\n  \"text\": \"The Envoy dynamic cluster discovery and health checking system is implemented across multiple layers in the envoyproxy/envoy repository. At the core, the CDS (Cluster Discovery Service) subscription mechanism is handled by CdsApiImpl (source/common/upstream/cds_api_impl.h/cc), which inherits from both CdsApi and SubscriptionBase. This class manages the gRPC subscription to cluster resources and callbacks (onConfigUpdate, onConfigUpdateFailed) that handle cluster updates.\\n\\nThe CdsApiHelper (source/common/upstream/cds_api_helper.h/cc) provides supporting functionality for the CDS API, while OdCdsApiImpl (source/common/upstream/od_cds_api_impl.h/cc) implements the On-Demand Cluster Discovery Service for dynamic cluster provisioning.\\n\\nThe cluster manager update logic is orchestrated by ClusterManagerImpl (source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h/cc), which manages cluster lifecycles and integrates with CDS. The ClusterDiscoveryManager (source/common/upstream/cluster_discovery_manager.h/cc) handles on-demand cluster discovery callbacks and discovery status tracking. ClusterUpdateTracker (source/common/upstream/cluster_update_tracker.h/cc) tracks the state of cluster updates, and ClusterFactoryImpl (source/common/upstream/cluster_factory_impl.h/cc) creates cluster instances from protobuf configurations.\\n\\nThe actual cluster and host implementations are in upstream_impl.h/cc. ClusterImplBase is the base class for all cluster types, managing cluster configuration, initialization, and member endpoints. HostImplBase implements the Host interface with health status tracking through multiple mechanisms: health check flags (FAILED_ACTIVE_HC, DEGRADED_ACTIVE_HC), EDS health status, and outlier detection flags. Hosts maintain references to HealthCheckHostMonitor and Outlier::DetectorHostMonitor through setHealthChecker() and setOutlierDetector() methods.\\n\\nActive health check scheduling is implemented through a multi-level architecture. The HealthCheckerFactory (source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h/cc) creates health checker instances for specific configurations, while HealthCheckerImplBase (source/extensions/health_checkers/common/health_checker_base_impl.h/cc) provides the base class for all health checkers. The key scheduling mechanism is the nested ActiveHealthCheckSession class, which manages interval timers (interval_timer_) and timeout timers (timeout_timer_) for health check scheduling. When HealthCheckerImplBase::start() is called, it begins scheduling health checks at configured intervals.\\n\\nSpecific health checker implementations include:\\n- HttpHealthCheckerImpl (source/extensions/health_checkers/http/health_checker_impl.h/cc): HTTP-based health checks\\n- TcpHealthCheckerImpl (source/extensions/health_checkers/tcp/health_checker_impl.h/cc): TCP health checks\\n- GrpcHealthCheckerImpl (source/extensions/health_checkers/grpc/health_checker_impl.h/cc): gRPC health checks\\n- Redis health checker and Thrift health checker implementations\\n\\nHealth check events are logged through HealthCheckerEventLogger (source/common/upstream/health_checker_event_logger.h/cc), which records transitions in host health status. The HealthDiscoveryService (source/common/upstream/health_discovery_service.h/cc) integrates health checkers with endpoint discovery.\\n\\nOutlier detection integration is implemented in OutlierDetectionImpl (source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.h/cc). The DetectorImplFactory creates detectors for clusters based on configuration. Outlier detection works in tandem with active health checking - hosts are marked with FAILED_OUTLIER_CHECK and other outlier-related flags that affect their overall health status.\\n\\nSupporting infrastructure includes:\\n- SubscriptionBase and SubscriptionFactoryImpl: Provide the subscription framework used by CdsApiImpl\\n- LoadStatsReporter: Reports load statistics from endpoints\\n- EdsClusterImpl and LedsClusterImpl: Implement cluster types that use Endpoint Discovery Service for dynamic endpoint updates\\n- Configuration and validation components in server/config_validation/ and server/admin/\\n\\nThe integration flow: CdsApiImpl receives cluster updates from the control plane, ClusterManagerImpl processes these updates through ClusterFactoryImpl, which creates ClusterImplBase instances. At the core, the CDS (Cluster Discovery Service) subscription mechanism is handled by CdsApiImpl (source/common/upstream/cds_api_impl.h/cc), which inherits from both CdsApi and SubscriptionBase. This class manages the gRPC subscription to cluster resources and callbacks (onConfigUpdate, onConfigUpdateFailed) that handle cluster updates.\\n\\nThe CdsApiHelper (source/common/upstream/cds_api_helper.h/cc) provides supporting functionality for the CDS API, while OdCdsApiImpl (source/common/upstream/od_cds_api_impl.h/cc) implements the On-Demand Cluster Discovery Service for dynamic cluster provisioning.\\n\\nThe cluster manager update logic is orchestrated by ClusterManagerImpl (source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h/cc), which manages cluster lifecycles and integrates with CDS. The ClusterDiscoveryManager (source/common/upstream/cluster_discovery_manager.h/cc) handles on-demand cluster discovery callbacks and discovery status tracking. ClusterUpdateTracker (source/common/upstream/cluster_update_tracker.h/cc) tracks the state of cluster updates, and ClusterFactoryImpl (source/common/upstream/cluster_factory_impl.h/cc) creates cluster instances from protobuf configurations.\\n\\nThe actual cluster and host implementations are in upstream_impl.h/cc. ClusterImplBase is the base class for all cluster types, managing cluster configuration, initialization, and member endpoints. HostImplBase implements the Host interface with health status tracking through multiple mechanisms: health check flags (FAILED_ACTIVE_HC, DEGRADED_ACTIVE_HC), EDS health status, and outlier detection flags. Hosts maintain references to HealthCheckHostMonitor and Outlier::DetectorHostMonitor through setHealthChecker() and setOutlierDetector() methods.\\n\\nActive health check scheduling is implemented through a multi-level architecture. The HealthCheckerFactory (source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h/cc) creates health checker instances for specific configurations, while HealthCheckerImplBase (source/extensions/health_checkers/common/health_checker_base_impl.h/cc) provides the base class for all health checkers. The key scheduling mechanism is the nested ActiveHealthCheckSession class, which manages interval timers (interval_timer_) and timeout timers (timeout_timer_) for health check scheduling. When HealthCheckerImplBase::start() is called, it begins scheduling health checks at configured intervals.\\n\\nSpecific health checker implementations include:\\n- HttpHealthCheckerImpl (source/extensions/health_checkers/http/health_checker_impl.h/cc): HTTP-based health checks\\n- TcpHealthCheckerImpl (source/extensions/health_checkers/tcp/health_checker_impl.h/cc): TCP health checks\\n- GrpcHealthCheckerImpl (source/extensions/health_checkers/grpc/health_checker_impl.h/cc): gRPC health checks\\n- Redis health checker and Thrift health checker implementations\\n\\nHealth check events are logged through HealthCheckerEventLogger (source/common/upstream/health_checker_event_logger.h/cc), which records transitions in host health status. The HealthDiscoveryService (source/common/upstream/health_discovery_service.h/cc) integrates health checkers with endpoint discovery.\\n\\nOutlier detection integration is implemented in OutlierDetectionImpl (source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.h/cc). The DetectorImplFactory creates detectors for clusters based on configuration. Outlier detection works in tandem with active health checking - hosts are marked with FAILED_OUTLIER_CHECK and other outlier-related flags that affect their overall health status.\\n\\nSupporting infrastructure includes:\\n- SubscriptionBase and SubscriptionFactoryImpl: Provide the subscription framework used by CdsApiImpl\\n- LoadStatsReporter: Reports load statistics from endpoints\\n- EdsClusterImpl and LedsClusterImpl: Implement cluster types that use Endpoint Discovery Service for dynamic endpoint updates\\n- Configuration and validation components in server/config_validation/ and server/admin/\\n\\nThe integration flow: CdsApiImpl receives cluster updates from the control plane, ClusterManagerImpl processes these updates through ClusterFactoryImpl, which creates ClusterImplBase instances. Each cluster initializes health checkers via HealthCheckerFactory, which creates the appropriate health checker type (HTTP, TCP, gRPC). These health checkers schedule active checks using interval/timeout timers in ActiveHealthCheckSession. Host health transitions trigger callbacks that update the host's health status, influence load balancing decisions, and are recorded in health check event logs. Outlier detection runs in parallel, ejecting hosts based on configurable thresholds, with detection status visible through host flags and health status.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
